I'm glad we're transitioning immediately into original territory now that the new team is fully established. We had our fun making callbacks and homages with Afterlife, but the mistake too many remake/sequel films make is getting stuck retreading old ground and forgetting to make anything new. This trailer instantly shows us that won't be a problem. It's also nice that the old Ghostbusters are sticking around, but I think that after being mentored by them for a little while, the new team will be strong enough characters by the end of this movie to carry the franchise on their own. I'll never say no to having Ray, Winston, and Venkman around, but it feels comforting to know that they're just a bonus addition to an already strong cast, not a nostalgia crutch. Objectively speaking, the actors aren't going to be around forever, and it's good to know that when they, too, pass on, the franchise name will still be in good hands.
